									 										 											 												Simple Button Trading setup : ï¿½ Button trading as the name suggests will trigger trade based on your command (click on the button). This can be applied on any AFL and it would not affect the primary logic of AFL, but rather would give you an option to trade manually too !. Sometimes due to the internet or other connectivity issues, we tend to miss trades when using algo bridge, Button trading can compensate that loss to a greater extent. Whenever you notice a particular signal has been skipped/ignored due to any reason, ï¿½click a button to take that trade and that would help you take that position. ï¿½ Button trading is also ï¿½particularly good starter for those who have no knowledge about amibroker and are starting to learn. You can place trades using the button and It would trigger trade via bridge instantly. How Button trading works : We basically have Four buttons : ï¿½ Buy: When clicked, triggers a Buy position. Sell: Exits the open Buy Position. Short: When clicked, triggers a fresh Short position. Cover: Exits the open Short position. ï¿½ You can also trade in peer scripts or in options by manually entering Strike price, option type, and expiry in parameters. ï¿½ Caution : If you are bearish on a particular script and expect it to fall down, then don't click on the Sell button, that just exits open buy position. To sell a script first is called short, and hence click on the short button, which would trigger a fresh Short position. ï¿½ Remember Sell and Cover button only exits open long and short positions respectively. To initiate a fresh buy/sell position click on Buy/short respectively. 									 									 										 											 												Multi time frame Supertrend. This AFL set up is for those conservative traders who prefer fewer trades but need more confirmation to reduce the possibilities of losses and enhance their winning accuracy. ï¿½ In this AFL set up, a User gets 4 custom time frames to compare the trend, and based on confirmation in all 4 time frames a trade is triggered. A user can select how many time frames he/she wants to check if a user just wants to check 2 or 3 timeframes that are also possible and a max of the 4-time frames will be possible. A user can set up any time frame and input will be in seconds (not in minutes) Ex : If the user sets 60, 300,900,3600 in time frame 1,2,3,4 respectively then the signal will be triggered after checking 1 min, 5min,15min, and 1 hour. So when the super trend generates a signal in all 4-time frames, only then the trade will be triggered. The parameters of Supertrend are customizable. ï¿½ Buy Logic: When Supertrend generates a Buy signal. Short logic: When Supertrend generates Short signal. Target: There are 2 targets, 1st target will exit 50% of the position and the remaining position will go on till target 2. There is a special trailing SL between Target 1 and Target 2 to lock your profits. These targets can be set in 2 ways : Points: Specific points from entry Percentage: Specific percentage from Entry. SL: There are 2 types of SL : Points: Specific points from entry Percentage: Specific percentage from Entry. ï¿½ ï¿½ Key Features : Scan Enabled. Works on both Intraday and positional mode. Backtest enabled. Fully automated. 2 targets with trailing SL enabled. 2 types of custom SL available. User can define as many time frames as he wants. All time frames are completely customizable. The long-only and short only mode available. Trade entry, no entry, and square off all timing can also be defined. Dashboard to check live trade status on chart enabled. ï¿½ Caution: Since this AFL compares multiple time frames before delivering the result, it will scan stocks much slower than those AFL where only a 1-time frame is used to generate entry and exit signal. Make sure you use a good local/virtual machine to handle this load. We suggest using a machine with at least 8GB RAM. ï¿½ Learn about this AFL here :											 										 										 											 												Back test Report 																																													 								 																																												 								 				 			 			 			 									 										 											Description 										 										 											Backtest Reports 										 										 											Reviews 										 										 											FAQs 										 									 									 										 											 												    This strategy uses 3 super-trend to enter and exit. Entry: When all 3 super-trend gives buy signal/sell signal, only then the trade will be taken in that direction. Exit: When all 3 super-trend gives sell signal/buy signal only then the trade will be taken in that direction. This is an exit and reverse strategy i.e. as the trend changes, the trade will also change and continue, Meaning at any time position will be open. Example: If the strategy generates Buy signal, and say 100 shares were bought, on next exit signal, There will be 2 trades of 100 shares : A sell to Square-off previous Buy position, and A short to initiate a new short position. Meaning, Buy and Cover would come together and sell and short would come together. However, the strategy has the option to disable the long/short position. When Long is disabled, the only short position will be initiated and squared-off at reversal. When Short is disabled, only Long position will be initiated and squared-off at reversal. Note: Since super-trend is a repainting indicator, it is advised to take a trade at the close of the candle(candle completion) to avoid entry in fake signals. Features : Works on any time frame All 3 super trend parameters can be customized Scan feature enabled. Auto-code integrated for 100% automated trading setup. Backtest Enabled. You can use 1, 2, or all 3 super trends together. Dashboard to showcase current position status. Customizable Target and SL. Switch between Intraday and Positional trade Easily. Trade entry, no entry after and square off time can also be customized. 											Backtest Reports 										 										 											Reviews 										 										 											FAQs 										 									 									 										 											 												average price (VWAP) is the ratio of the value traded to total volume traded over a particular time horizon (usually one day). It is a measure of the average price a stock traded at over the trading horizon. But to understand VWAP in a simple manner here is a video from marketvision which explains VWAP in plain english which brings more visibility on the hidden facts of VWAP. 											Reviews 										 										 											FAQs 										 									 									 										 											 												 Simply put, an area of support is where the price of an asset tends to stop falling, and an area of resistance is where the price tends to stop rising. But traders really need more information about support and resistance beyond those simple definitions before they attempt to make trading decisions based on those areas in a chart.  To use support and resistance effectively, youï¿½first need to understand how asset prices typically move, so you can then interpret support and resistance from that framework. You also need to be aware that there are different types of support and resistance, such as minor andï¿½major/strong. Minor levels are expected to be broken, while strong levels are more likely to hold and cause the price to move in the other direction.   Using Trendlines  EURUSD 1-Minute Chart with Various Types of Support and Resistance.ï¿½MT4 Support and resistance are highlighted with horizontal or angled lines, calledï¿½trendlines. If the price stalls and reverses in the same price area on two different occasions in succession, then a horizontal line isï¿½drawn to show that the market is struggling to move past that area.  In an uptrend, the price makes higher highs and higher lows. In aï¿½downtrend, the price makes lower lows and lower highs. Connect the highs and lows during a trend. Then extend that line out to the right to see where the price may potentially find support or resistance in the future.  These simple lines highlight trends, ranges, and other chart patterns. They provide traders with a visual of how the market is currently moving and what it could do in the future. 																																												 								 				 			 			 			 									 										 											Description 										 										 											Backtest Reports 										 										 											Reviews 										 										 											FAQs 										 									 									 										 											 												The MACD is one of the most popular and broadly used indicators for Forex trading. The letters M.A.C.D. is abbreviation for Moving Average Convergence Divergence. The MACD indicator, which requires Moving Averages as its input, falls into the group of the lagging indicators.ï¿½ The basic function of the MACD Forex indicator is to discover new trends and to help identify the end of current trends. There are various ways to gauge the signals generated by MACD, and many traders use their own unique settings and methods around thisï¿½trading indicator. More and Buy)   ï¿½ ï¿½ Optimised EMA This is the modified version of Normal EMA crossover with lots of math logic to optimize entry and exit. Firstly we check the distance between the crossover and the candle formed at the time of the crossover, if the distance is more, we ignore the signal as It tends to spoil our Risk-reward ratios. Also, we initiate a trade when High/low of the candle which gave crossover is broken. Stoploss can be in terms of Points or percentage or crossover of moving average. The target can be in terms of Points or Percentage, we have 2 targets here. At tgt1 partial exit is done, and remaining is trailed till tgt2 is achieved. ï¿½ Ex: If the buy is generated at 215, Letï¿½s say 100 shares are bought at 215 rs, and tgt1 is 219 and tgt2 is 222 So at 219, say 40 shares will be booked, rest 60 shares will be trailed till 222 is reached. However, if you donï¿½t want 2 targets, you can change it to a single target also. We can customize the range of distance between Crossover and candle, Moving averages, square off time. We can also set no trade after a certain time, beyond which, no fresh entries will be triggered. ï¿½ The strategy works very well in trending days in bluechip stocks. ï¿½  Watch the Entire explanation of the strategy here :   watch the working of this strategy in Live markets here :    											 										 										 											 												Back test Report 									 																																													 								 																																												 								 				 			 			 			 									 										 											Description 										 										 											Backtest Reports 										 										 											Reviews 										 										 											FAQs 										 									 									 										 											 												    What is a moving average? A moving average (MA) is a widely used indicator in technical analysis that helps to gauge the direction of the current trend of the market. Types of moving averages- There are several different types of moving averages available in the market(simple, weighted, time series, VIDYA, exponential) but professional traders use only two types of moving averages namely simple moving average, also called SMA and exponential moving average, also called EMA. How is a moving average calculated? A moving average is calculated by simply calculating the mean of the underlying asset over a period of n intervals. Mean is computed by dividing the sum of ï¿½nï¿½ values by number of values ï¿½nï¿½.    Let us understand this with the help of an example given below- Let us take a population of 13 datasets. Out of that population we will select a sample of 10 datasets as shown below. The moving average for period 10 is given as-    But there is a slight difference between simple mean and moving averages. Moving averages have a moving tendency as the dataset grows. Hence if we add another number ï¿½5ï¿½ to the dataset and keep the period constant at 10 then the new moving average will discard the oldest data point which in this case is 15. The entire scenario is depicted as follows-    Simple Moving average (SMA)- A simple moving average is the simple moving mean calculation that we talked about before. It divides the sum of the values by the total number of values. As said before, simple moving average also discards older values as newer values come into existence. The formula of SMA is same as mean or MA-    The calculation of SMA with period 10 is shown below Plotting a Simple Moving Average on a chart- The chart above is of Reliance Industries limited. There are two lines running on the chart, one is green and the other one is red. The green moving average is 20-SMA and the red moving average is 50-SMA. As you can see the red moving average is moving slower as compared to the green moving average with respect to fluctuations in price. This is because the green moving average is 20-SMA, it comprises of 20 data points only and has less lag whereas the red moving average is 50-SMA, it comprises of 50 data points and has more lag due to this. Exponential Moving average (EMA)- The exponential moving average is slightly different than SMA, its calculation differs a lot and that is why when EMA is plotted, it is slightly different than SMA. The formula for EMA is given below- The most important difference between a simple moving average and an exponential moving average is that SMA treats all prices in the ï¿½nï¿½ period same whereas EMA gives more weightage to the most recent prices out of ï¿½nï¿½ prices. Plotting an Exponential Moving Average on a chart- The same company ï¿½Relianceï¿½ is taken in this example as well. The green line is the 20EMA and the red line is the 50EMA. The data points are also same as the previous example for SMA, but youï¿½ll notice that SMA and EMA are different. Basically both EMA and SMA are used to give us buy or sell signals but EMA gives us the signal a few candles before only. This is due to the fact that it gives more weightage to the recently formed candles. What do Moving Averages tell you and how to use them for trading? Moving averages lag current price action because they are based on past prices; the longer the time period for the moving average, the greater the lag. Thus, a 200-day MA will have a much greater degree of lag than a 20-day MA because it contains prices for the past 200 days. The length of the moving average to use depends on the trading objectives, with shorter moving averages used for short-term trading and longer-term moving averages more suited for long-term investors. Using either SMA or EMA is the choice of the trader. The trader can use either SMA or EMA depending on his/her trading compatibility and his/her comfort. Following are a few ways in which professional traders use the moving averages- The 50-day, 100-day and 200-day MAs are widely followed by investors and traders, with breaks above and below these moving averages considered to be important trading levels. Positional traders use the combination of 20-day, 50-day, 100 day and 200-day moving averages. If 20-MA crosses above the 50-MA it signals a bullish movement whereas if the 20-MA crosses below the 50-MA it signals a bearish movement. Both these crossovers are calledï¿½Golden Crossovers. Short term or intraday traders use combinations of 5-MA, 8-MA, 13-MA and 20-MA. Moving averages are also seen as important support and resistance levels from where the prices might bounce back. 									 									 										 											 												This is a very advanced setup, one of the most popular concepts based on Price action and very effective in the Indian market. The AFL marks Swing High and Swing low of any time frame and takes trade based on Higher high or lower low breakouts. Trade set up : For Long entry: The Script should have higher low and when the previous high is broken, we BUY. For Short entry: The script should have a lower high and when the previous low is broken, we short. Target: There are 2 types of Target and there are 2 targets with trailing SL. Points: Specific points from Entry. Percentage: Specific Percentage from Entry.ï¿½ ï¿½ Stoploss: There are 3 types of Stoploss Points: Specific points from Entry. Percentage: Specific percentage from Entry.ï¿½ï¿½ Swing High/low: For Long position, previous swing low will be SL and for Short position, previous swing high will be SL. Key Features : Scan Enabled Backtest enabled. Fully automated AFL Runs on all time frameï¿½ Swing set up can be customized. Swing differences can be customized. Intraday and Positional mode enabled. Trade entry, no entry, and square off time can be customized. Disable long or short option available. 2 targets with custom trailing SL enabled. 3 types of SL with custom exit enabled. Dashboard to provide live trade status on chart enabled. Whitelabel option enabled. ï¿½ Didn't understand? 											Backtest Reports 										 										 											Reviews 										 										 											FAQs 										 									 									 										 											 												Advanced Range breakout setup. Advanced range breakout is a mix of Initial range break out and Custom range break out pattern. It has many customizable parameters that make it the most advanced range breakout system. ï¿½ You can define the range of any time desired time frame at your convenience. Once the range is defined, now we have 3 options for the user to check the range. Check High- low range: This is the conventional way of marking high and low of the stock price in a defined time, and mark them as a range. Check Open and Close: Instead of marking High and Low, you can also mark Open and close of the defined time and mark it as a range. Only open price: Mark only opening price as a reference and use it as breakout reference. You can also add a buffer to this range to refine your entries. Trade Logic : One a range is defined by the above parameters, the trade will be triggered on the following logic : Long entry: If the upper range + Buffer(if any) is broken, Buy. Short entry: If the lower range ï¿½ Buffer (if any) is broken, Short. ï¿½ Target: There are 2 targets, 1st target will exit 50% of the position and the remaining position will go on till target 2. There is a special trailing SL between Target 1 and Target 2 to lock your profits. These targets can be set in 2 ways : Points: Specific points from entry Percentage: Specific percentage from Entry. SL: There are 3 types of SL : Range: For long position, Use lower range ï¿½ buffer (if any) as SL. And for Short positions use upper range + buffer (if any) as SL. Points: Specific points from Entry. Percentage: Specific percentage from Entry. Max trades per day can also be defined, the AFL will not produce signals, once max trades per day is triggered. ï¿½ Key Features : Scan Enabled. This is purely intraday strategy only, it won't work on Positional mode. Backtest enabled. Fully automated. 2 targets with trailing SL enabled. 3 types of custom SL available. The range can be defined in 3 ways. Max trade per day can be defined. The long-only and short only mode available. Trade entry, no entry, and square off all timing can also be defined. Custom buffer for entry and exit available. Dashboard to check live trade status on chart enabled. ï¿½ Learn about Advanced range breakout AFL here :											 										 										 											 												Back test Report 										 											Backtest Reports 										 										 											Reviews 										 										 											FAQs 										 									 									 										 											 												People who succeed at day trading do three things very well:ï¿½ They identify intra-day trading strategies that are tried, tested.ï¿½ They are 100% disciplined in executing those strategies.ï¿½ They stick to a strict money management regime. Intraday traders have an arsenal of strategies but one very popular Intraday strategy called the ï¿½Open High Low Strategyï¿½ has had reasonably good results as is evidenced by the popularity. In this strategy, Buy signal is generated when a Stock or Index has same value for Open and Low, while Sell signal is generated when it has same value for Open and High. Prabhudas Lilladherï¿½s Mobile App (www.plindia.com/plmobileapp) presents this strategy live in its Scanners section. It is ideal that traders watch this screen from 9.15 and then decide the trades at 9.45 AM depending on which stocks continued their momentum in the same direction as at open. One can keep the stop loss as the previous day close rates . In any case Allow no more than a 1% move against you from your entry point. Once momentum fades and buyers are thinning out, take your profit. Ideal Strategy Using PL Mobile App Create a watchlist from the scrips appearing in the Long and Short section of the Open High Low Strategy at 9.15. Note down the previous dayï¿½s high lows as well as pivot levels, all of which are available in the PL Mobile App. Till 9.45 , see the behavior in the scripï¿½s price moves, movement in Open Interest in case it is a derivatives security as well and of course, whether any news is there on these stocks. If you want to go through charts, please do so as well on the Mobile App which provides you tick by tick charting https;//plindia.com/plmobileapp 9.45 AM: Entry for Long:Note down previous dayï¿½s High price and after market opens today, wait for the price to breakout yesterdayï¿½s high and when broken check if Todayï¿½s Open = Todayï¿½s Low at that time, if Yes go long with Stop loss as todayï¿½s Low price. 9.45 AM: Entry for Short Note down previous dayï¿½s Low price and after market opens today, wait for the price to breakdown yesterdayï¿½s low and when broken check if Todayï¿½s Open = Todayï¿½s High at that time, if Yes go Short with Stop loss as todayï¿½s High price. Exit: Exit at End Of the Day or a defined stop loss. If your stock hits a new low for the day (long trades) or new high for the day if you are short, exit the position. The new highs or lows are also reported by the Mobile App in the scanners section. A day trade is intended for initial moves, so there is no purpose in widening stops to accommodate a stock moving in the wrong direction. Get out if the stock breaks a low (or high if short) as you can reenter the trade if it triggers again. Traders can use the Resistance Support levels in the PL Mobile App as points of reference when deciding the stop loss ï¿½ with support level / resistance level breaks defined as stops OR in terms of absolute amounts, lets say 0.5% ï¿½ Ideally, you should run the strategy on at least 5 scrips for a well diversified approach											 										 										 											 												Back test Report 										 											 												Super scalping AFL is one of the most advanced AFL available in India. With 20+ flexible parameters to choose from, this AFL becomes completely customizable and one of the favorite tools for both Trader and Investor. ï¿½ Logic: This AFL keeps scalping custom quantity of stock/future/options as the user decides, making range bound movement highly profitable phase. First choose the start date, time, and till what time you want to scalp. Also, you can choose if you want to scalp for intraday or for the long term. Trading Type: Here you can select what type of scalping you want to do. If you are looking to scalp in uptrend movement select Buy-Sell mode and If you are looking to the scalp in downtrend movement select Short-cover type. Trading Mode: You can switch between the Intraday and Positional strategy. First Entry level: Here you can decide from what price you want to start scalping a specific script. Scalping Target point: Here you can decide at what price interval it should keep scalping. Stop-loss level: This is the level where the stock will stop scalping and square off all open positions. Max Open Quantity: Here you can decide how many shares max you want to go up to while scalping. Position method: we have three choices here : ï¿½A. Incremental: It keeps increasing position during each scalp. ï¿½B. Constant: Keep's scalping by constant quantity. ï¿½C. Custom: You can decide the custom quantity on all levels. We have given 20 levels ï¿½ Display settings: There are 10 display settings you can enable disable dashboard your setting status trade status on the chart quantity management display and many other features. ï¿½ Key levels: Here you can visualize many key levels like Todayï¿½s high and low Todayï¿½s mid-level Yesterdayï¿½s high low Weekly high low Monthly high low Last month high low. These levels can help you decide and accumulate shares at a better price. ï¿½ How to use this strategy? For Positional trading: If you want to trade positionally, and wish to buy and hold shares for the long term, this scalping strategy can help you accumulate stocks at a better price and also help you make some money via scalping. For Intraday trading: Find a range-bound stock and keep scalping and make most of the choppy market. ï¿½ To understand the entire AFL see the video and learn how to scalp. 									 									 										 											 												Advanced Open High low set up Advanced OHL setup is a step ahead of normal Open High low concept It has many customizable parameters that make it the Advanced OHL setup. ï¿½ You can filter entry based on 3 logics : Normal: Just checks if Open = High or Open = Low and based on it, we take trades. Previous day Close: For long position, Open of the current day should be above the previous day close, and for a short position, the current day open should be below the previous day close. Previous day High/low: For long position, Open of the current day should be above previous day High, and for a short position, current day open should be below previous day low. Trade Logic : Long entry: If Open = Low, Buy at the open of next candle. Short entry: If Open = High, Short at the open of the next candle. ï¿½ Target: There are 2 targets, 1st target will exit 50% of the position and the remaining position will go on till target 2. There is a special trailing SL between Target 1 and Target 2 to lock your profits. These targets can be set in 2 ways : Points: Specific points from entry Percentage: Specific percentage from Entry. SL: There are 3 types of SL : First candle High/low: For long position, the First candle open is SL. And for Short positions also First candle open is SL. Points: Specific points from Entry. Percentage: Specific percentage from Entry. ï¿½ Key Features : Scan Enabled. This is purely intraday strategy only, it won't work on Positional mode. Backtest enabled. Fully automated. 2 targets with trailing SL enabled. 3 types of custom SL available. Open high low filter can be defined in 3 ways. The long-only and short only mode available. Trade entry, no entry, and square off all timing can also be defined. Dashboard to check live trade status on chart enabled. ï¿½ Learn about Advanced OHL ï¿½AFL here :											 										 										 											 												Back test Report AFL (Read More and Buy)   ï¿½August 25, 2019 Posted by:ï¿½PurpleTrades Category:ï¿½AFL No Comments    Get this AFL at INR 2999 only.  Buy Now  Supertrend with Martingale systemï¿½AFLï¿½as the name suggests is just the mixture of Supertrend and martingale system. So when Supertrend generates BUY/SELL Signal, it would take a trade and continue until the next trade comes and at next trade, it will exit the previous position and reverse the trade (Exit and reverse). However, since the Martingale system is also involved, now AFL will keep monitoring P/L. In case, the trade gives loss, we double our quantity in the next trade and keep doing this until we make profits. Once the trade turns positive, the next trade would again be having the initial quantity to start the entire process all over again. This AFL Has 2 types of martingale: Arithmetic:ï¿½In this system, Instead of doubling every time we lose, we simply add quantity as per arithmetic progression. Ex: We Buy 10 shares of X Stock and it goes against us, we exit and reverse 20 shares, and say it goes against us, then we exit and reverse 30 shares(not 40 shares) So arithmetic series would be : 10, 20, 30, 40, 50ï¿½ï¿½ï¿½. Geometric:ï¿½As the name suggests, we have geometric progression or basically doubling shares every time we lose. Ex: We Buy 10 shares of X Stock and it goes against us, we exit and reverse 20 shares, and say it goes against us, then we exit and reverse 40ï¿½ shares So Geometric series would be : 10,20,40,80,160ï¿½ï¿½ï¿½. A user can choose between these two types of martingale system. The AFL looks like this on Amibroker Letï¿½s explore the features/ parameters of this AFL: It has supertrend ATR to adjust as per your preferred requirements If you use Supertrend (10,3) you have to fill ATR Multiple: 3 ATR Period: 10 AFL has options to customize trade time: Activate Intraday: To choose if you want to trade Intraday/delivery based trading. Trade entry fromï¿½: If day starts, from what time should AFL start accepting signals. In case you give this as 9:45 am, so any trade between 9:15 to 9:45 am will be discarded, as you wanted to take trade only post 9:45 am. Trade entry upto:ï¿½Till what time fresh entry should be accepted.If you fill this as 2:30 pm, any fresh trade after 2:30 pm will be ignored however the open positions initiated before 2:30 pm will be still valid and running. Trade exit: This will generate exit on all open positions, say you fill this as 3:10pm, so all open positions will be squared of at 3:10 pm sharp. ï¿½ AFL has Risk management tools: Stoploss: In case you want to keep SL in the system, you can customize SL in percentage here. If Buy entry was at 100rs and you keep SL as 1%, SL would be set at 99rs, irrespective of supertrend give sell signal or not. Target: In case you want to keep Target in the system, you can customize Target in percentage here. If Buy was at 100rs and you keep the target as 1%, Target would be set for 101rs, irrespective of supertrend gives sell signal or not. Trailing SL: You can also keep trailing SL in percentage. To choose the number of shares per trade we have 3 options: Trade quantity: You can choose the number of shares you wish to start trading with. If you fill this as 30, per script that you run this AFL on, 30 shares will be bought/sold, and as per martingale system the quantity will double to 60, in case you lose the first trade and so on OR Quantity using Exposure: Incase you dynamically wnt to allocate the number of shares, you can do so by filling in this exposure tab. If you fill 10000, then it would buy/sell shares worth 10000rs. If X share is of 500, 20 shares will be bought/sold. If Y share is of 1000, 10 shares will be bought/sold. And as per martingale rule, if we lose 1st trade, the exposure in 2nd trade will be 20,000 and so on. OR Quantity using SL: This feature will dynamically adjust your position size as per SL defined. Say you define SL as 1000rs and in SL tab above as 1% for the stock of 100rs, it means SL of 1rs. Thus 1000 shares will be bought/sold as per this SL based system. (Note :ï¿½You cannot choose all the three together, you have to choose your quantity only as per one of the above-mentioned method and rest you have to set to 0, in case you fill 2 or3 of the quantity method it would give you an error) Day profit limit: You can set a limit on profit per script per day. If you fill this as 1000, then after all the trades in a script in a day, if the net gain is 1000, it would stop trading in that script. Day loss limit: you can set a limit on loss per day. If you fill this as 1000, then after all the trades in a script in a day, if net loss is 1000, it would stop trading in that script. Misc: Message board: This will show you whatï¿½s happening with your position, your current MTM per script, how much profit is booked for the day, when did the last signal come and other details. Button trading:ï¿½we have also added four buttons LE, LX, SE, SX corresponding to Lon entry, long exit, short entry, and short exit respectively In case you manually want to place a trade at any given time, you on click on any of the button and corresponding trade would be triggered. Trade Intrabar: If its Yes, it would take a trade on the same candle on which entry had come, if its Candle completion, it would wait for the candle to complete and then take a trade on opening of nxt candle Strategy Tag: you can give a tag to your strategy. Once all of these settings are done, your AFL is ready for trading. Get this AFL at INR 2999 only.  Buy Now  ## AFL will be delivered in 1 working day to your registered email address (Monday- Friday) (Warning: Martingale based systems can be profitable if used with proper risk-management tools, else this system can give huge losses. It is always advised to place Limit order and not market orders to avoid the losses due to spread in ask-bid. Purpletrades will not be responsible for any loss that you face using this system, consult your financial advisor before using this setup) Find it difficult to understand?
